\"validatingDispatcher.callHook\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain is implemented through a sophisticated architecture spanning multiple packages:\\n\\n## Core Plugin Entry Points\\n\\n**MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): The plugin implements admission.MutationInterface, with the Admit() method delegating to the generic Webhook.Dispatch() method. Registered as \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\" and created via NewMutatingWebhook().\\n\\n**ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): The plugin implements admission.ValidationInterface, with the Validate() method delegating to Webhook.Dispatch(). Registered as \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\" and created via NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook().\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**Webhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go): The abstract base class that both plugins inherit. Contains the Dispatch() method which retrieves webhooks from the source and invokes the specific dispatcher. Also provides ShouldCallHook() to determine if a webhook should be invoked based on namespace/object selectors and rules matching.\\n\\n**Interfaces** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go): Defines the Dispatcher interface and WebhookInvocation structure that describes how to call a webhook.\\n\\n## Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\n**mutatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go): Implements the Dispatcher interface for mutating webhooks. The Dispatch() method iterates through hooks sequentially, calling callAttrMutatingHook() for each. Handles reinvocation context to support webhook re-invocation when objects are modified. Applies JSON patches to the object and aggregates audit annotations and warnings.\\n\\n**validatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go): Implements the Dispatcher interface for validating webhooks. The Dispatch() method collects all relevant hooks, then invokes them in parallel using goroutines. Each hook is called via callHook() independently, with errors collected and returned together.\\n\\n## Request/Response Handling and Aggregation\\n\\n**admissionreview** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go): Handles the creation and verification of admission review objects. CreateAdmissionObjects() creates AdmissionRequest/Response objects in the appropriate version (v1 or v1beta1) based on the webhook's declared versions. VerifyAdmissionResponse() validates the webhook response, checking UID matches, ensuring patch/patchType consistency, extracting audit annotations and warnings, and returning the aggregated AdmissionResponse.\\n\\n## Webhook Configuration Management\\n\\n**Configuration Managers** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/): Manages dynamic webhook configurations via informers. mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager implement the generic.Source interface, providing lists of webhook accessors from MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources respectively.\\n\\n## Webhook Accessors\\n\\n**WebhookAccessor** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go): Abstract interface providing common access patterns to both mutating and validating webhook definitions. Includes methods to get webhook properties, REST clients, namespace/object selectors, match conditions, and rules. Implementations wrap v1.MutatingWebhook and v1.ValidatingWebhook.\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n**Reinvocation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go): Tracks which webhooks have been invoked and may be reinvoked if mutations occur during the admission chain.\\n\\n**Match Conditions** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/): Compiles and evaluates CEL expressions for webhook match conditions.\\n\\n**Error Handling** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/): Provides error conversion for webhook responses.\\n\\n## Overall Admission Chain Integration\\n\\n**Admission Chain** Plugin Entry Points\\n\\n**MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): The plugin implements admission.MutationInterface, with the Admit() method delegating to the generic Webhook.Dispatch() method. Registered as \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\" and created via NewMutatingWebhook().\\n\\n**ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): The plugin implements admission.ValidationInterface, with the Validate() method delegating to Webhook.Dispatch(). Registered as \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\" and created via NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook().\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\n**Webhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go): The abstract base class that both plugins inherit. Contains the Dispatch() method which retrieves webhooks from the source and invokes the specific dispatcher. Also provides ShouldCallHook() to determine if a webhook should be invoked based on namespace/object selectors and rules matching.\\n\\n**Interfaces** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go): Defines the Dispatcher interface and WebhookInvocation structure that describes how to call a webhook.\\n\\n## Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\n**mutatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go): Implements the Dispatcher interface for mutating webhooks. The Dispatch() method iterates through hooks sequentially, calling callAttrMutatingHook() for each. Handles reinvocation context to support webhook re-invocation when objects are modified. Applies JSON patches to the object and aggregates audit annotations and warnings.\\n\\n**validatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go): Implements the Dispatcher interface for validating webhooks. The Dispatch() method collects all relevant hooks, then invokes them in parallel using goroutines. Each hook is called via callHook() independently, with errors collected and returned together.\\n\\n## Request/Response Handling and Aggregation\\n\\n**admissionreview** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go): Handles the creation and verification of admission review objects. CreateAdmissionObjects() creates AdmissionRequest/Response objects in the appropriate version (v1 or v1beta1) based on the webhook's declared versions. VerifyAdmissionResponse() validates the webhook response, checking UID matches, ensuring patch/patchType consistency, extracting audit annotations and warnings, and returning the aggregated AdmissionResponse.\\n\\n## Webhook Configuration Management\\n\\n**Configuration Managers** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/): Manages dynamic webhook configurations via informers. mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager implement the generic.Source interface, providing lists of webhook accessors from MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources respectively.\\n\\n## Webhook Accessors\\n\\n**WebhookAccessor** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go): Abstract interface providing common access patterns to both mutating and validating webhook definitions. Includes methods to get webhook properties, REST clients, namespace/object selectors, match conditions, and rules. Implementations wrap v1.MutatingWebhook and v1.ValidatingWebhook.\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n**Reinvocation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go): Tracks which webhooks have been invoked and may be reinvoked if mutations occur during the admission chain.\\n\\n**Match Conditions** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/): Compiles and evaluates CEL expressions for webhook match conditions.\\n\\n**Error Handling** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/): Provides error conversion for webhook responses.\\n\\n## Overall Admission Chain Integration\\n\\n**Admission Chain** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go): The chainAdmissionHandler executes handlers in sequence, supporting both Admit() and Validate() operations.\\n\\n**Reinvocation Handler** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go): Wraps the admission chain to handle reinvocation of eligible webhooks when mutations occur.\\n\\n## Call Flow\\n\\nFor mutating webhooks: Admit() → Webhook.Dispatch() → mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() → [for each hook] ShouldCallHook() → callAttrMutatingHook() → CreateAdmissionObjects() → webhook call → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → apply patches\\n\\nFor validating webhooks: Validate() → Webhook.Dispatch() → validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() → [parallel for each hook] ShouldCallHook() → callHook() → CreateAdmissionObjects() → webhook call → VerifyAdmissionResponse() → aggregate results\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
